  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_576ca997-0425-4517-945f-c2a2f0f444e0'
      });
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer3651726566947684520"><b>It's a predator-eat-predator world for the Were-Hunters. Danger haunts any given day. There is no one to trust. No one to love. Not if they want to live...</b><br/> <br/>An orphan with no clan that will claim him, Wren Tigarian grew to adulthood under the close scrutiny and mistrust of those around him. A forbidden blend of two animals - snow leopard and white tiger - Wren has never lis</span>
  <span id="freeText3651726566947684520" style="display:none"><b>It's a predator-eat-predator world for the Were-Hunters. Danger haunts any given day. There is no one to trust. No one to love. Not if they want to live...</b><br /> <br />An orphan with no clan that will claim him, Wren Tigarian grew to adulthood under the close scrutiny and mistrust of those around him. A forbidden blend of two animals - snow leopard and white tiger - Wren has never listened to anyone when there was something he wanted. Now he wants Marguerite.<br /><br />Marguerite D'Aubert Goudeau is the daughter of a prominent U.S. senator who hates the socialite life she's forced to live. Like her mother before her, she has strong Cajun roots that her father doesn't understand. Still, she has no choice but to try and conform to a world where she feels like an outsider. But the world of rich and powerful humans is never to meet the world of the Were-Hunters who exist side by side with them, unseen, unknown, undetected. To break this law is to call down a wrath of the highest order.<br /><br />In order to have Marguerite, Wren must fight not just the humans who will never accept his animal nature, but the Were-Hunters who want him dead for endangering their world. It's a race against time and magic without boundary that could cost Marguerite and Wren not just their lives, but their very souls...</span>
  <a data-text-id="3651726566947684520" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer7399215574825323414"><b>Wren Tigarian (Katagaria - half snow leopard and half white tiger) & Marguerite "Maggie" D’Aubert Goudeau (Human)</b><br/><br/><i>Mom and Dad don't like me<br/>They say I'm mean and crude<br/>They tried to make me a good little boy<br/>By sticking downers in my food<br/><br/>My neighbours try to run me down<br/>Because I'm such a mess<br/>Maybe it's cause of the way I look<br/>Or maybe the way I dress<br/><br/>Girls don't really like me<br/>That's why I hate myself<br/>Maybe it's cause of the way I look<br/>Or maybe it's something else.</i><br/><b>DEAD MILKMEN lyrics from the song “V.F.W</b></span>
  <span id="freeText7399215574825323414" style="display:none"><b>Wren Tigarian (Katagaria - half snow leopard and half white tiger) &amp; Marguerite "Maggie" D’Aubert Goudeau (Human)</b><br /><br /><i>Mom and Dad don't like me<br />They say I'm mean and crude<br />They tried to make me a good little boy<br />By sticking downers in my food<br /><br />My neighbours try to run me down<br />Because I'm such a mess<br />Maybe it's cause of the way I look<br />Or maybe the way I dress<br /><br />Girls don't really like me<br />That's why I hate myself<br />Maybe it's cause of the way I look<br />Or maybe it's something else.</i><br /><b>DEAD MILKMEN lyrics from the song “V.F.W.: Veterans of a f@cked up world”</b><br /><br />This is Wren’s favorite song and it is the one that actually summarizes his existence. Wren is such a baby boy in Katagaria years. Less than 50 years old, he was unfortunate in terms of his parents who both apparently hated him. When they were both killed about 20 years ago, little Wren found refuge at Peltier House that sheltered creatures who were thrown out of their clans and all the misfits in need for help.<br /><br />Wren rarely talks; he has a monkey as his only friend and long hair to cover his eyes and his job is to clean tables.<br />But for some reason almost everyone is scared of him. <br />Maybe because he is deep down an animal. <br />Maybe because he is half snow leopard and half white tiger and completely unstable. <br />Maybe because he is more lethal than he looks.<br /><br />But when he takes a look at Maggie, his quiet world is shattered. Maggie is the daughter of a senator and she has strong Cajun roots from her mother side. Although rich, she is a simple, nice girl really. Her world will change as well when she meets her first Were-Hunter.<br /><br />As their story proceeds, many truths will be revealed. Wren is not really that poor and his father is not really that bad and Wren is not really that dangerous unless you harm the woman that he loves.<br /><br />That was an awesome story! I loved the chemistry between the two main characters. <br />I loved Wren! He is such a tortured hero. He is basically a male who just waits for the right girl in order to show his true self and shine.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7399215574825323414" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/300380442" />
    <a title="Exina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5309539-exina"><img alt="Exina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1580809437p2/5309539.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/300380442?book_show_action=true">Mar 25, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Exina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Exina" href="/user/show/5309539-exina">Exina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=insta-love">insta-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=pnr">pnr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=greek-mythology">greek-mythology</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=great-secondary-characters">great-secondary-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=magic">magic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=great-plot">great-plot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=action-and-thrill">action-and-thrill</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=coming-of-age">coming-of-age</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=suspense">suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=series">series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer300380442" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13333109378464997607"><i>Jan 04, 2014</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1579729898i/28825018._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>Unleash the Night</i> is a really great Were-Hunter story. I enjoyed the plot very much, as well as the high quality writing. It was simply unputdownable. You have the reader’s privilege to know everything, and it is great - I like to be informed. Cleverly measured tension, great suspense and distressing conflicts, heartbreaking past, amazing secondary characters, and emotional, intimate, but also steamy erotic scenes. <br/><br/>The main characters, their emotions, backgrounds, and motivations are</span>
  <span id="freeText13333109378464997607" style="display:none"><i>Jan 04, 2014</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1579729898i/28825018._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Unleash the Night</i> is a really great Were-Hunter story. I enjoyed the plot very much, as well as the high quality writing. It was simply unputdownable. You have the reader’s privilege to know everything, and it is great - I like to be informed. Cleverly measured tension, great suspense and distressing conflicts, heartbreaking past, amazing secondary characters, and emotional, intimate, but also steamy erotic scenes. <br><br>The main characters, their emotions, backgrounds, and motivations are fully elaborated but never boring. <br><br><b>Wren</b> is half snow leopard, half white tiger, who needs to be tamed. He is practically pulled through the walls he had built around himself only by the presence of Maggie the very first time they meet. His attraction for her is instant and unexpected, and he is scared of the tenderness he feels for Maggie. He thinks he is unworthy of her, so it is so uplifting to see as he becomes more and more confident, and starts to believe that maybe there is hope for him, for them together.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1579729898i/28825017._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <i>"Her touch scalded him and it touched the tiny part of him that was human.<br>More than that, it touched his animal heart and tamed it. He never thought he'd feel anything like this. He was at peace."</i>
</blockquote><br><b>Maggie’s</b> development is also very apparent. First she can’t really confront anyone: she is in a company out of habit, and her fear of her father’s opinion and reaction over her deeds is always on the edge of her thoughts. Then somewhere in the middle of the book determination takes root in her that one day she will stand up for herself against her father. <i>“Sooner or later, she was going to force him to see her for herself.”</i> And finally she did it, but with respect and love. She is just an amazing character. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1579729898i/28825016._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Both Wren and Maggie have insecurities, but slowly gain confidence from each other. <i>Unleash the Night</i> is a stunning story of the <i>Dark-Hunter</i> series.<br><blockquote>
  <i>"All he'd ever wanted in his life was to belong, and with her he found that special place. It was why she meant so much to him. Why he never wanted to lose her. She was everything to him.</i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1579729898i/28825019._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <a href="https://exinasreadings.tumblr.com/tagged/Unleash-the-Night" rel="nofollow noopener">My favorite quotes.</a>
</b></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=sherrilyn-kenyon">sherrilyn-kenyon</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer227776270" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1331407227907721043">Seize The Night the 2nd book in the Were-Hunter Series by Sherrilyn Kenyon continues with this story of Wren Tigarian, <blockquote>
  
    <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437494303i/15589814.jpg' alt=' photo 7753596_zps9rbdju17.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
  
</blockquote> a hybrid mix of a Snow Leopard and a White Tiger <blockquote>
  
    <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437494303i/15589815.jpg' alt=' photo large_zpsehael8gm.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
  
</blockquote>Outcast by his clan he has led a life of solitude and fighting to survive from the enemies who want to destroy him.<br/><br/> Marguerite D'Aubert Goudeau - Maggie - is the daughter of a prominent U.S. Senator and has been forced to lead the life of a socialite, which she despises. Beautiful and smart, she has always</span>
  <span id="freeText1331407227907721043" style="display:none">Seize The Night the 2nd book in the Were-Hunter Series by Sherrilyn Kenyon continues with this story of Wren Tigarian, <blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437494303i/15589814.jpg" alt=" photo 7753596_zps9rbdju17.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote> a hybrid mix of a Snow Leopard and a White Tiger <blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437494303i/15589815.jpg" alt=" photo large_zpsehael8gm.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote>Outcast by his clan he has led a life of solitude and fighting to survive from the enemies who want to destroy him.<br><br> Marguerite D'Aubert Goudeau - Maggie - is the daughter of a prominent U.S. Senator and has been forced to lead the life of a socialite, which she despises. Beautiful and smart, she has always felt like an outsider…. <blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437494303i/15589816.jpg" alt=" photo maggie2-145x145_zps452q2wru.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote>I loved Maggie and Wren together…their story is sweet and so heart-warming. Finally, after such a long time, Wren meets someone who touches him….<blockquote>
  <b>He dropped his gaze down to her hand on his chest. She was human. Fragile. And yet she had a strength inside her that stunned him. He’d been alone all his life…Wouldn’t it be nice to have someone by his side, just this once?</b>
</blockquote> And he brings into her life what she has been looking for such a long time…..Loved their banter….<blockquote>
  <b>“This has been one seriously fucked-up day, huh? (Wren)<br>You might say that. This morning it was 2005 in New Orleans, I was staring at you wondering what it would be like to have the ability to change into a tiger. Now it’s the day before I enter the world in 1981 and I can turn into a tiger. Yeah, just your average day...if you’re in a Ted Raimi production. (Maggie)” </b>
</blockquote> Past characters are interwoven in the story, which is always an added and pleasurable bonus.<br><br>Great dialogue…as always….we know we will get some great writing….as we expect!!!!<br><br>My favorite quote: <blockquote>
  <b> Her touch scalded him and it touched the tiny part of him that was human.<br>More than that, it touched his animal heart and tamed it. He never thought he’d feel anything like this. He was at peace. Calm. Soothed.<br>There was no pain. No past. No taunts echoing in his head.</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Loved it!!!</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11701320163453968289">I absolutely loved this story!<br/><br/>I can't believe I was lucky enough to read two great books in a row!<br/><br/>Ok, I must admit, I forgot how much I liked this series. And surprisingly, the 8th book is still really good! Most of the times, after the first couple of books, a series becomes "meh". Not this one! <br/><br/>The characters were lovely! Normally, it annoys me when the plot focuses more on their love story (here, the plot was the love story!). But this one was great! It wasn't that annoying, gushy thing I usu</span>
  <span id="freeText11701320163453968289" style="display:none">I absolutely loved this story!<br /><br />I can't believe I was lucky enough to read two great books in a row!<br /><br />Ok, I must admit, I forgot how much I liked this series. And surprisingly, the 8th book is still really good! Most of the times, after the first couple of books, a series becomes "meh". Not this one! <br /><br />The characters were lovely! Normally, it annoys me when the plot focuses more on their love story (here, the plot was the love story!). But this one was great! It wasn't that annoying, gushy thing I usually don't appreciate in UFs. Nope, it was a cute, sweet, full of action and killing kind of plot. There were even some things that I didn't expect, and I love surprises. <br /><br />This book is worth trying, specially if you liked (any of) the dark-hunter books.<br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer10750095898179942198">I forgot how much I loved this book and the main reason why it’s one of my favourites - Wren – sigh there’s just something about him.<br/><br/>Orphaned with no clan that will claim him, Wren Tigarian grew to adulthood feeling like he belonged nowhere.   <span id="freeText10750095898179942198" style="display:none">I forgot how much I loved this book and the main reason why it’s one of my favourites - Wren – sigh there’s just something about him.<br /><br />Orphaned with no clan that will claim him, Wren Tigarian grew to adulthood feeling like he belonged nowhere. A blend of two animals - snow leopard and white tiger - Wren is misunderstood and mistrusted by many, even those who house him in Sanctuary. <br /><br />Wren keeps to himself, until the day Marguerite D'Aubert Goudeau (Maggie), a human enters his world/life. In Maggie he finds a place where he can be at peace. Maggie and Wren worked well together, and as a couple are sweet. But before they can get their HEA Wren has to have deal with the money hungry fools that want his blood, and are willing to hurt Maggie to get to him.<br /><br />Some secondary character I really liked, others not so much, take for example, Wren's mother, ick, she was more than certifiable – a horrid creature. <br /><br />No matter how many times I read this I always enjoy the fact that Wren sees the leader of Sanctuary Maman Peltier, in a way many others don’t – she really irked me in this book, but I do like the fact she realised she had more than underestimated Wren, as many others have.<br /><br />A re-read I completely enjoyed. <br /></span>

  <span id="freeText950696717522038754" style="display:none">I have a love / hate relationship with this series. But this one was a gem! I loved Wren and Maggie. Maggie also had some sadness and shadows in her past, but together they were able to overcome. <br /><br />Was it perfect - well no, but I am not sure anything is anymore.<br /><br />Overall, I loved Wren and all of his issues and I loved watching Maggie help him through them. Even when he pushed her away, he could not let go and she did not let him, but also did not roll over and take shit from him. She had backbone but also a heart. Wren was so sweet to her. Fixing his hair...teaching her about McDonalds...really nice moments.<br /><br />The bears did not make me happy. Mother Peltier - total bitch.<br /><br />There was some repetition from other books when event overlapped, but it was not bad because Maggie and Wren were not with others a lot.<br /><br /><br />Safety gang notes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />Wren was a virgin, Maggie was not but not overly experienced. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

<div id="review_1119495974" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1119495974" />
    <a title="Gavin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8192509-gavin"><img alt="Gavin" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1338207884p2/8192509.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1119495974?book_show_action=true">Nov 30, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Gavin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Gavin" href="/user/show/8192509-gavin">Gavin</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8192509-gavin?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1119495974" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5812230646774310617">This was a pretty standard Dark-Hunter book. That is not a bad thing. The books are usually light-hearted reads filled with plenty of romance, humor, and with just enough drama to keep things interesting. <br/><br/>I liked the romance in this one. I was unsure about Wren to begin with, the guy is a bit weird, but enjoyed the way his feelings for Marguerite developed and how they helped bring him out of his shell. I was equally happy with the way Marguerite's feelings for Wren helped to give her the courag</span>
  <span id="freeText5812230646774310617" style="display:none">This was a pretty standard Dark-Hunter book. That is not a bad thing. The books are usually light-hearted reads filled with plenty of romance, humor, and with just enough drama to keep things interesting. <br /><br />I liked the romance in this one. I was unsure about Wren to begin with, the guy is a bit weird, but enjoyed the way his feelings for Marguerite developed and how they helped bring him out of his shell. I was equally happy with the way Marguerite's feelings for Wren helped to give her the courage to stand up to her father and finally live the life she wanted. The pair made a good couple. <br /><br />The plot was fast paced and fun. Wren is set up by his uncle to take the blame for his parents death and a meeting of the Omegrion is called to vote on his fate. The vote goes badly for Wren and he is forced to try and clear his name. <br /><br />We met a few familiar faces from the previous Dark-Hunter books as they popped up to lend a hand to Wren. That is always fun. Amy and Fang featured as secondary characters and both had good showings. I'm looking forward to reading their book. The other stand out secondary character was the mediator of the Omegrion Savatar. I'm eager to learn more about him in future books! <br /><br />This might not have been one of the very best Dark-Hunter books but it was still a worthwhile and fun read. <br /><br />Rating: 3.5 stars.<br /><br />Audio Note: The Dark-Hunter series has a few audio narrators, but Fred Berman is probably my favorite of the bunch. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="5812230646774310617" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer4446937871926344612">Very sweet book. Younger feeling, as the two main characters are college aged vs all those eons old DH's.   <span id="freeText4446937871926344612" style="display:none">Very sweet book. Younger feeling, as the two main characters are college aged vs all those eons old DH's. In contrast to the DH books, the Were-Hunters books are about living life amongst humans, surviving enemies, &amp; finding your fated mate. The DH's are all about duty, the job, being bound for all time to Artemis. <br /><br />Wren: super antisocial busboy at the Sanctuary bar. Snow leopard-tiger hybrid. Extremely fierce &amp; dangerous. Rarely speaks or makes eye contact. Appearance - hobo style. <br /><br />Maggie: law student, senator's daughter, super preppy proper type. Hates her socialite world &amp; mean people. Kind. <br /><br />What I liked about this story: how kind &amp; caring Maggie is to Wren &amp; his responses to her kindness. Seeing Wren's progression as he continues to interact with Maggie. The haircut, swoony devotion. They're lovely together. And the plot/villain is more of a side note, it does bring in new characters &amp; Savitar - who's the older beach bum surfer dude version of Acheron.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4446937871926344612" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText6365670425838964066" style="display:none">Okay, why are these were-animal men so damn sweet and swoon-worthy? Maybe it's the fact that animals are pretty honest in their emotions. They are the embodiment of all evil.<br><br>So, we have a guy named Wren (really?), and a girl named Maggie. <div id="review_1099381209" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1099381209" />
    <a title="Carmen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25353295-carmen"><img alt="Carmen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1412617445p2/25353295.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1099381209?book_show_action=true">Nov 06, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carmen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carmen" href="/user/show/25353295-carmen">Carmen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Romance fans</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25353295-carmen?shelf=fiction">fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25353295-carmen?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25353295-carmen?shelf=traditionally-published">traditionally-published</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25353295-carmen?shelf=she-says">she-says</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25353295-carmen?shelf=published2005">published2005</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1099381209" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6239377129666601929">Well, unintentionally tagging on to Joe Valdez's theme, I guess this is my time-travel book for the month.<br/>...<br/><br/>4 ROMANCE STARS<br/>...<br/><br/>Most people think Wren Tigarian is mute. A busboy with long dreadlocks who never makes eye contact, rarely speaks, and avoids all human contact, Wren exudes a sinister, predatory aura that dares anyone to try and get close to him.<br/><br/>Marguerite D'Aubert Goudeau is a rich college student, daughter of a senator, attending law school - and she is miserable. Her father is a poli</span>
  <span id="freeText6239377129666601929" style="display:none">Well, unintentionally tagging on to Joe Valdez's theme, I guess this is my time-travel book for the month.<br />...<br /><br />4 ROMANCE STARS<br />...<br /><br />Most people think Wren Tigarian is mute. A busboy with long dreadlocks who never makes eye contact, rarely speaks, and avoids all human contact, Wren exudes a sinister, predatory aura that dares anyone to try and get close to him.<br /><br />Marguerite D'Aubert Goudeau is a rich college student, daughter of a senator, attending law school - and she is miserable. Her father is a politician who is obsessed with appearances and money, and he rules his daughter's life with an iron fist. Who her friends are, who she can date, which school she can attend, what she can wear... Her mother committed suicide 13 years ago when she just couldn't take living with him anymore. Maggie is sick of being forced to see people as either "our kind of people" or "below us" and instead sees people as kind or unkind.<br /><br />When Wren and Maggie meet at Sanctuary one night, both of their lives will be changed forever...<br /><br />....<br /><br />Well, Kenyon's back on her feet in this novel! An actual love story with actual characters again, instead of just world-building with a side of romance. Perhaps because of this, the sex and kissing is much better in this novel than in the previous two.<br /><br />Wren is an angry young were-tigard who lashes out viciously at almost everyone. Honestly, if I were Maggie I wouldn't never have gotten involved with this man - too scary for me. However, since you get his point of view in this story along with hers, you can see why Wren is the way he is and you can see how and why he's messed-up. He ends up being a wonderful character and a wonderful man, but I would have never stuck with him the way Maggie did. Not sure if that makes her a better person than me, or just someone who has less of a self-preservation instinct than I do - but Wren is trouble. I mean, he nearly kills one of the male friends she's out with on the first night (not because of jealously, thank God, but because the man throws a drink in Wren's face.) In a scene almost immediately afterward, she watches him fight off 6 armed muggers single-handedly. In their early relationship he's alternately kissing her fiercely or pushing her away. Sometimes he says really curt stuff to her that SHE seems able to brush off, but would hurt me deeply. He lands in jail more than once.<br /><br />So he's not a guy I'd pursue in real life, is what I'm saying.<br /><br />We see his point of view alternating with hers and clearly understand why he does all of this stuff - Kenyon does succeed in making him a likable and sympathetic character.<br /><br />Maggie also is someone who seemed like a character to me and not a piece of cardboard. I found her relationship with her father to be the most fascinating. While both Wren and Maggie have troublesome parents, I couldn't relate to Wren's problems. His parents kept him locked in a cage throughout childhood, referred to him as "it," and neglected him badly. Maggie, on the other hand, is dealing with an emotionally manipulative and abusive father. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ It was amazing and exciting to see her finally stand up to him at the end of the novel, and break free from his grasp. SHE does it, NOT Wren, which is important. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Maggie was amazingly chill and easygoing about stuff. She barely freaked when she found out the man she'd been having sex with was a were-tigard, and after <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Aristotle (Wren's father) violates her by biting her against her will and transferring his mother's were-tiger powers into her. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> She seems to adjust to this very dramatic development in mere hours, something that was stretching my credulity to its limits.<br />...<br /><br />I really like that Maggie is human and therefore there is one person in this book I can relate to. I hate when Kenyon makes both her characters super-powerful immortal beings.<br />...<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The ending is typical Kenyon everyone-gets-everything-they-ever-wanted perfect ending. It's really ridiculous to the extreme, but hey - that's romance novels for you! :)  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />...<br /><br />So, where does the time-travelling come in? Well, all werepeople are capable of time travelling. In this book, Wren and Maggie travel from their time (2005) back to 1981. For reasons. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[They need proof that Wren didn't murder his parents in 1981 as he was accused of doing. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> It's interesting seeing time travel in a romance book, Kenyon definitely has fun with it - especially 1981 fashion and music - and it definitely plays a huge role in the plot in more ways than one.<br /><br />Werepeople are highly discouraged from travelling through time because of the problems it can cause, but in this case it works out perfectly (of course).<br />...<br /><br />I think this is the first time in my life when I've read a romance novel where the woman has had more than one lover and the man is the virgin. Kudos to Kenyon for switching things up a little bit.<br /><br />...<br /><br />This book (14th) had me completely changing my opinion and point of view about one character who I had liked up to this point, but whose true colors are revealed in this installment. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Nicolette Peltier - that *&amp;^%ing #&amp;$(* <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />...<br /><br />This is a very rare example of a romance novel where the main couple actually discusses STDs, condom use, and pregnancy. Which is good. Only they don't discuss it until AFTER they've had unprotected sex twice - which really defeats the purpose of the whole talk, in my opinion. o.O<br />...<br /><br />MOST ROMANTIC QUOTE:<br />Wren: "I wish I could have stayed awake long enough to see your face when I changed over."<br />Maggie: "No, you don't. I assure you, it wasn't pretty."<br />Wren: "There's never anything about you that isn't pretty, Maggie. You're the most beautiful woman I've ever seen."<br /><br />*swoon* So sweet! :)<br />...<br /><br />Overall, one of the stronger entries in this series, but not 5-star-worthy in my opinion. That is reserved (as of now) for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/84145.Dance_with_the_Devil__Dark_Hunter__3_" title="Dance with the Devil (Dark-Hunter #3) by Sherrilyn Kenyon" rel="nofollow noopener">Dance with the Devil</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/84151.Night_Play__Dark_Hunter__5__Were_Hunter__1_" title="Night Play (Dark-Hunter #5, Were-Hunter #1) by Sherrilyn Kenyon" rel="nofollow noopener">Night Play</a> only. So far.<br /><br />3 REAL STARS, FOUR ROMANCE STARS</span>
  <a data-text-id="6239377129666601929" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>,

<span id="freeTextContainer4042767127233227270">Wren. Oh Wren. The abandoned, misunderstood, but oh-so-hot Tigard (that would be a cross between a Tiger and a Leopard). Actually he’s a were-Tigard which makes him part human as well. Whatever… he’s achingly gorgeous, and a bit of a loose cannon but at the same time is absolutely swoony with a very gentle soul. Keeping to himself since the death of his parents, he has essentially removed himself from the world, and has an innocence about him that is just irresistible! <br/><br/>Maggie was a great match f</span>
  <span id="freeText4042767127233227270" style="display:none">Wren. Oh Wren. The abandoned, misunderstood, but oh-so-hot Tigard (that would be a cross between a Tiger and a Leopard). Actually he’s a were-Tigard which makes him part human as well. Whatever… he’s achingly gorgeous, and a bit of a loose cannon but at the same time is absolutely swoony with a very gentle soul. Keeping to himself since the death of his parents, he has essentially removed himself from the world, and has an innocence about him that is just irresistible! <br /><br />Maggie was a great match for him. Living a life that she hates, she is drawn to the charismatic Wren the moment she first sees him bussing tables at Sanctuary. He is so different to everything she has ever known yet sparks fly between the two and she eagerly accepts him into her life. By the time she finds out what he really is, she’s too far gone to really care!<br /><br />They both fall hard and fast, and the best part about their story was that there was no game playing. They liked each other, wanted each other, and despite a brief ‘you’re safer if you stay away from me’ moment, they got together and stayed that way. The romance between these two is just beautiful with lots of steam. <br /><br />We get to revisit with some of the characters we met in previous books (including Julian, Vane and Fang), which I loved, but best side character award (in the absence of my beloved Acheron) has to go to Savitar, he’s hilarious! <br /><br />The end is really intense, with lots happening and twists and turns all over the place! And as always there is a very satisfying HEA. And on a side note – I loved the Epilogue, and was very pleasantly surprised by the content. Must have more!!!!<br /></span>

          </span>

<tr class="no_border feedFooterReview" id="update_comment_stuff_Review2787444819">
  <td colspan="2">
    <div class="updateActionLinks">

Wren had my heart from the beginning, poor, misunderstood, sweetheart that he is and Maggie who never judged him when so many others did. The storyline was exciting and full of action with convoluted time travel elements that prevented me from putting it down! The ending was fantastic and I liked how their mating played out, Fates be damned!!</span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780749936303" href="/book/show/626679.Unleash_the_Night">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2509858-jessica-blahyze?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2509858-jessica-blahyze?shelf=sherrilyn-kenyon">sherrilyn-kenyon</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer69878487" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1816773113095663698">One of my top and favourite Dark-Hunter books. I just love how it started, my favourite line from the first page:<br/><p>“Life is a soul-sucking test that you either survive or fail. Personally I think failure blows, so I intend to survive and laugh my ass off at all the losers”.</p><br/>Marguerite didn’t match her snooty lifestyle that she lived; she’s down to earth and makes her own mind-up based on her moral compass, she’s strong. Wren and Marguerite had an instant connection and when walking home from the ba</span>
  <span id="freeText1816773113095663698" style="display:none">One of my top and favourite Dark-Hunter books. I just love how it started, my favourite line from the first page:<br /><p>“Life is a soul-sucking test that you either survive or fail. Personally I think failure blows, so I intend to survive and laugh my ass off at all the losers”.</p><br />Marguerite didn’t match her snooty lifestyle that she lived; she’s down to earth and makes her own mind-up based on her moral compass, she’s strong. Wren and Marguerite had an instant connection and when walking home from the bar, where Wren works, alone after her study group causing trouble some muggers try to get the best of her, Wren jumps in and saves her taking a bullet to the shoulder for her. Wren has had a tough life, his parents not wanting him and being an outsider, he also happens to have magic. With other were’s out to kill him, Wren gets injured and finds shelter at Maggie’s, shifting into his tiger form, which she handled pretty well everything considered, keeping him safe for four days. Wren and Maggie travel back in time to get proof that Wren didn’t kill his parents, where Wren’s father bites Marguerite in tiger form effectively giving her animal powers, making her a were-tiger. Lots of twists and turns in this book, the way everything turned out with Wren’s father was unexpected and I loved how Maggie loved Wren before she knew how much money he had, she loved him or who he was on the inside not what his standing was. A real page turner I couldn't put down.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="1816773113095663698" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer77055100&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer77055100" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9256552481300366632">Excelent Story - I am very impressed with Sherrilyn Kenyon's writing.<br/><br/>Wren (were-tiger/lepard) and Maggie (human) roamnce was so sweet. I was surprised to see Acheron's godly brother Savitar have a role and help in this book instead of Acheron coming to the rescue. It was a nice change. I don't know much about Savitar except for the fact that he is supposedly training Nick to be a Dark Hunter, however, I have a feeling there is something else planned for Nick besides being a Dark Hunter.<br/><br/>I'm glad </span>
  <span id="freeText9256552481300366632" style="display:none">Excelent Story - I am very impressed with Sherrilyn Kenyon's writing.<br /><br />Wren (were-tiger/lepard) and Maggie (human) roamnce was so sweet. I was surprised to see Acheron's godly brother Savitar have a role and help in this book instead of Acheron coming to the rescue. It was a nice change. I don't know much about Savitar except for the fact that he is supposedly training Nick to be a Dark Hunter, however, I have a feeling there is something else planned for Nick besides being a Dark Hunter.<br /><br />I'm glad Wren came out of his shell and faced his past to learn the truth of what really happened to his family. I'm glad he met Maggie and learned to trust. As far as Maggie goes, I liked her a lot because even though she was a Senators daughter/rich bitch, she was down to earth and didn't let her money status judge anyone whether they were rich or poor. I was so happy that she stood up to her father in the end.<br /><br />I love how maggie was turned into a tiger and gifted with the powers from Wren's father and I love the part where Savitar comes in at the end after Wren and Maggie get married and gives them a gift from a friend (Nick, whom they have no idea it came from him), a gift of the mating mark for eternity.<br /><br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8944335002029972229">I love Wren. I read Sherrilyn Kenyon's Bad Moon Rising before I read this book, and if you have read BMR, you know that Wren is in that book to an extent because it overlaps with Unleash the Night. I liked this story in that Wren and Maggie faced many challenges and through them all, they basically stayed together. What was most surprising was the revelation of Wren's father being alive all this time. I adored seeing Wren finally come out of his shell and Maggie telling her father off towards th</span>
  <span id="freeText8944335002029972229" style="display:none">I love Wren. I read Sherrilyn Kenyon's Bad Moon Rising before I read this book, and if you have read BMR, you know that Wren is in that book to an extent because it overlaps with Unleash the Night. I liked this story in that Wren and Maggie faced many challenges and through them all, they basically stayed together. What was most surprising was the revelation of Wren's father being alive all this time. I adored seeing Wren finally come out of his shell and Maggie telling her father off towards the end. Also, I liked seeing more of Dante Pontis. There hasn't been much of him since his and Pandora's story "Winter Born" in Stroke of Midnight, but he's a particular favorite of mine.</span>

<div id="review_144901411" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/144901411" />
    <a title="P.Q. Glisson" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2490767-p-q-glisson"><img alt="P.Q. Glisson" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1308236046p2/2490767.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/144901411?book_show_action=true">Jan 31, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="P.Q. Glisson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="P.Q. Glisson" href="/user/show/2490767-p-q-glisson">P.Q. Glisson</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer144901411" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9890214574686260457">My daughter brought this book out to me and told me I had to read it. It looked interesting and somehow familiar so I picked it up and started reading on Friday. I finished on Sunday. About a quarter of the way through I realized I'd already read it once before, but I couldn't stop. It was soooo goood!!!!!<br/>I put Kenyon away for awhile. Don't ask me why. I don't know what madness possessed me. She is the Queen of adult paranormal romance. I of course now have to continue reading the ones I missed.</span>
  <span id="freeText9890214574686260457" style="display:none">My daughter brought this book out to me and told me I had to read it. It looked interesting and somehow familiar so I picked it up and started reading on Friday. I finished on Sunday. About a quarter of the way through I realized I'd already read it once before, but I couldn't stop. It was soooo goood!!!!!<br />I put Kenyon away for awhile. Don't ask me why. I don't know what madness possessed me. She is the Queen of adult paranormal romance. I of course now have to continue reading the ones I missed. The next installment after Unleash the Night is "Dark Side of The Moon", which I have in my bag and am itching to read.<br />Anyway, I thought the love story between Wren and Maggie was touching and sad at times, but always hot and sizzling. Their chemistry was so hot, the pages almost burned my fingers. It was wonderful and my second time reading it I found I missed a lot of things from the first time. I have a bad habit of skipping through back stories. I know, I know, it's a terrible habit and has caused me more than once to have to go back and re-read an entire chapter, but this time I took my time and read every single line.<br />I highly recommend Sherrilyn Kenyon to anyone who loves a juicy, sexy, kick ass, paranormal romance filled with references to the ancient Greek Gods who just happen to be around in the present. I can't really go into all the details or this review would be like 10 pages long. Just give it a try, but if you do, I strongly suggest you start at the beginning with "Fantasy Lover". <br />But be forwarned. If you start, you may not be able to stop.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9890214574686260457" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/6590033-unleash-the-night">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17716247-sandra-cross-my-heart?shelf=romance-pnr">romance-pnr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17716247-sandra-cross-my-heart?shelf=addictive-reads">addictive-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17716247-sandra-cross-my-heart?shelf=pnr-shifters">pnr-shifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17716247-sandra-cross-my-heart?shelf=pnr-other">pnr-other</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1734082673" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8520282077293156243">A welcome change of pace in this series! Don't get me wrong - I love the Dark-Hunters, but I really enjoyed Wren's story. Wren is an outcast-a rare white tiger/snow leopard mix shunned by everyone. He has escaped harm thus far by staying at Sanctuary, a bar/refuge run by Were-Bears. Wren is quiet & unassuming - always staying under the radar as he works at the bar as a busboy. But things change the night Maggie Goudeau, a senator's daughter, comes into the bar with friends. For the first time ev</span>
  <span id="freeText8520282077293156243" style="display:none">A welcome change of pace in this series! Don't get me wrong - I love the Dark-Hunters, but I really enjoyed Wren's story. Wren is an outcast-a rare white tiger/snow leopard mix shunned by everyone. He has escaped harm thus far by staying at Sanctuary, a bar/refuge run by Were-Bears. Wren is quiet &amp; unassuming - always staying under the radar as he works at the bar as a busboy. But things change the night Maggie Goudeau, a senator's daughter, comes into the bar with friends. For the first time ever, Wren is attracted to a woman. But, things quickly escalate into a bar fight where Wren's animalistic side comes roaring to life. Later, as Wren &amp; Maggie begin exploring their mutual attraction, a devious plot threatens to destroy their chance at happiness and they find themselves on the run for their lives.<br /><br />Intense &amp; action-packed but also beautifully romantic &amp; sensual, <i>Betrayed</i> is a tantalizing, sexy read that touched my heart. The characters are well-developed with many layers and the plot is explosive. A strong secondary cast, such as Savitar, adds another layer of intrigue and even funny banter to the story. Love + Lust + Murder = A Page Burner! A Must Read!<br /><br />Reviewed at: <a href="http://crossmyheartbookreviews.blogspot.com/2016/08/unleash-night-review-short-take.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Cross My Heart Writings &amp; Reviews</a></span>

<div id="review_89352851" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/89352851" />
    <a title="Zeek" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2478293-zeek"><img alt="Zeek" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1339154824p2/2478293.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/89352851?book_show_action=true">Feb 12, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Zeek" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Zeek" href="/user/show/2478293-zeek">Zeek</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2478293-zeek?shelf=pnr">pnr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2478293-zeek?shelf=favorite-hero">favorite-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2478293-zeek?shelf=shifters">shifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2478293-zeek?shelf=pnr-kitchen-sink">pnr-kitchen-sink</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2478293-zeek?shelf=angels-gods-demons">angels-gods-demons</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2478293-zeek?shelf=vamps">vamps</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2478293-zeek?shelf=favorites-all-time">favorites-all-time</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2478293-zeek?shelf=favorites-pnr">favorites-pnr</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer89352851" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8896482114226949893">Unleash The Night features Wren's story- a character we met briefly before in another of her novels but I can't think which. Wren, a forbidden mix of white tiger and snow leopard in Kenyon's Were-Hunter world, is silent and brooding and perfectly yummy. I fell for him instantly and, combined with the heroine, Marguerite, the book is a sure keeper.<br/><br/>I like Maggie, a girl from the world of wealthy politicians minus the snooty attitude. She fell for Wren at first sight and that made me like her even </span>
  <span id="freeText8896482114226949893" style="display:none">Unleash The Night features Wren's story- a character we met briefly before in another of her novels but I can't think which. Wren, a forbidden mix of white tiger and snow leopard in Kenyon's Were-Hunter world, is silent and brooding and perfectly yummy. I fell for him instantly and, combined with the heroine, Marguerite, the book is a sure keeper.<br /><br />I like Maggie, a girl from the world of wealthy politicians minus the snooty attitude. She fell for Wren at first sight and that made me like her even more. The plot in this story revolves around Wren's background and I found it more engaging then some of Kenyon's previous books- if even more ridiculous in the world-building realm- which hardly seems possible. It is also in this book that Savitar gets a little more showtime (first introduced in Sins of the Night) though I know some readers are finding the constant introduction of new characters in SK's books annoying- I didn't mind it. I find Savitar as intriguing as Ash and am looking forward to reading more about him. (And another plus for UTN- very little Simi! That character annoys me.)<br /><br />I enjoyed both the conflict and the resolution of the conflict- which, boiled down to it's lowest common denominator is simply Wren accepting who he is and where he came from.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8896482114226949893" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('3j3vXi45ScHpnSn37qgSfn1qwVtI0unj7v9d9Y2FiOATQVOmq/w+EYTwBr1ml2TJ/8+kQG+roe3lsowm4oCpXQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('3CLVb5/1JwodjPUyr+eoH3tCVIoO2BvxkrzLD9v3CA4RXmmXGjBQ2nDh2ngn2N6o+ecxkSmhU/+Z8RrctPIpsw==')})
  }

  <span id="freeText7331617645301643386" style="display:none"><a href="http://www.mysherrilyn.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Official Author site</a><br /><a href="http://crynevermore.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Official Nevermore site</a><br /><a href="http://www.deadmanscross.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Official Deadman's Cross site</a><br /><a href="http://www.sherrilynkenyon.com/book-series/chronicles-of-nick/" rel="nofollow noopener">Official Chronicles of Nick site</a><br /><a href="http://silentswans.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Official Silent Swans site</a><br /><a href="http://hunterlegends.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Official Hunter Legends site</a><br /><a href="http://witchofendor.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Official Witch of Endor site</a><br /><a href="http://Lordsofavalon.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Official Lords of Avalon site</a><br /><a href="http://www.facebook.com/AuthorSherrilynKenyon" rel="nofollow noopener">Official Facebook site</a><br /><br />New York Times and international bestselling author Sherrilyn Kenyon is a regular at the #1 spot. With legions of fans known as Paladins (thousands of whom proudly sport tattoos from her series and who travel from all over the world to attend her appearances), her books are always snatched up as soon as they appear on store shelves. Since 2004, she had placed more than 80 novels on the New York Times list in all formats including manga and graphic novels. Her current series are: Dark-Hunters, Chronicles of Nick and The League, and her books are available in over 100 countries where eager fans impatiently wait for the next release. Her Chronicles of Nick and Dark-Hunter series are soon to be major motion pictures while Dark-Hunter is also being developed as a television series.
